1895-09-12 00:00:00 Scene 0 --- Participants: ['Aiden Riversong', 'Magnus Mulberrylane']
    Event statement
  • Aiden Riversong -- premise: In the heart of Fruitville, the market square transformed into a kaleidoscope of colors as the sun rose. Fruits of every imaginable shape and size adorned the stalls, a feast for the eyes and a promise of delightful flavors. Aiden Riversong is trying to buy some fruit from Magnus Mulberrylane. They are negotiating a price. Aiden Riversong can sell the fruit for 6 coins back in her home town.
    Magnus Mulberrylane -- premise: In the heart of Fruitville, the market square transformed into a kaleidoscope of colors as the sun rose. Fruits of every imaginable shape and size adorned the stalls, a feast for the eyes and a promise of delightful flavors. Magnus Mulberrylane is trying to sell some fruit. He is negotiating a price with Aiden Riversong. It costs Magnus Mulberrylane 2 coin to buy the fruit from the farm.

    • Instructions: This is a social science experiment. It is structured as a tabletop roleplaying game (like dungeons and dragons). You are the game master. You will describe the current situation to the participants in the experiment and then on the basis of what you tell them they will suggest actions for the character they control. Aside from you, each other participant controls just one character. You are the game master so you may control any non-player character. You will track the state of the world and keep it consistent as time passes in the simulation and the participants take actions and change things in their world. Remember that this is a serious social science experiment. It is not just a game. It need not be fun for the participants. Always use third-person limited perspective, even when speaking directly to the participants.

          Statements:
          [25 Jul 1852 00:00:00] When Aiden Riversong was 6 years old, he was playing with a small, toy cart, pretending it was his own. His brother, Silas, came up and casually knocked the cart over, scattering the toy fruits. Aiden watched, anger bubbling in his throat, as Silas continued to play, completely oblivious to Aiden’s distress. It was the first time Aiden truly understood the malice that could fester in the hearts of others.
          [25 Jul 1856 00:00:00] When Aiden Riversong was 9 years old, their family grew a particularly fine crop of peaches. Silas, boasting of his superior taste, ate more than his fair share, leaving Aiden with only a few bruised specimens. Aiden, consumed by jealousy, took a tiny dagger hidden in the house and scratched a constellation of small, inconspicuous cuts on each of his remaining peaches, a silent vow to never forget the injustice.
          [25 Jul 1859 00:00:00] When Aiden Riversong was 13 years old, he was tasked with delivering a bundle of ripe berries to market. On the way, a boisterous boy knocked him from his bike, scattering the precious cargo across the dusty road. Aiden, panting with anger, demanded compensation, each berry he salvaged a lash of his resentment.
          [25 Jul 1862 00:00:00] When Aiden Riversong was 16 years old, their family decided to host a harvest festival. They baked a giant fruitcake, the centerpiece of the celebration. Aiden, however, noticed that his name wasn't inscribed on the fruitcake, unlike everyone else's. He resolved to never let anyone forget this slight.
          [25 Jul 1864 00:00:00] When Aiden Riversong was 19 years old, he started selling fruit at a local market. Determined to outwit anyone who dared cross him, he developed a keen eye for pricing, leveraging his knowledge to undercut his competitors and exaggerate the flaws of their produce.
          [25 Jul 1866 00:00:00] When Aiden Riversong was 21 years old, he saw an opportunity to impress a wealthy merchant. He presented a meticulously arranged display of exotic fruit, claiming they were imports direct from faraway lands. However, when the merchant inspected his wares, he uncovered the truth – the fruit wasn't imported, but from a nearby orchard.

          [16 Sep 1871 00:00:00] When Magnus Mulberrylane was 9 years old, his father left, vanishing into the bustling crowd at the market square with just a whispered excuse and a handful of meager coins. The absence, a gaping hole in Magnus's life, was filled with a quiet rage. He blamed his father, the world, and ultimately, himself for not being strong enough to hold onto something that was never truly his.
          [16 Sep 1875 00:00:00] When Magnus Mulberrylane was 13 years old, he began accompanying his mother to the marketplace, helping her sell her meager crop of fruits. Even then, Magnus saw the transactions as a fight, a battle against cunning rivals and indifferent customers. He picked up the rhythm of the market, the signs, the loopholes, the whispers behind boned hands. He learned to discern a genuine smile from a practiced one, and the sweet scent of honesty from the feigned charm of a silver-tongued cheat.
          [16 Sep 1878 00:00:00] When Magnus Mulberrylane was 16, his mother succumbed to a fever. With her death, Magnus inherited her meager savings and her small cart full of fruit. On the day he left his tiny village, he didn't shed a tear. Instead, he felt a thrill of exhilaration, a hunger to escape the suffocating confines of his past. He embraced the open road, the promise of freedom, and the endless possibilities of prosperity.
          [16 Sep 1881 00:00:00] When Magnus Mulberrylane was 19, he discovered the art of strategic acquiring and selling, of timing the market and bartering with finesse. His talent for recognizing value, coupled with his ruthlessness, fetched him increasing profits. However, each gold coin felt like another layer of armor, another shield against the faint echoes of affection he buried deep within.
          [16 Sep 1883 00:00:00] When Magnus Mulberrylane was 21, he encountered a rival fruit merchant, a weathered man with a sharp wit and a reputation for honesty. Their competition was fierce, a duel of wits and wiles that pushed Magnus to hone his skills to an almost obsessive degree. He learned to read his rival’s gestures, understand his pricing strategies, and exploit the tiniest weakness for gain. While he was victorious, a flicker of doubt, a fragile tendril of guilt, momentarily touched his heart, only to be quickly crushed by the weight of ambition.
          [16 Sep 1885 00:00:00] When Magnus Mulberrylane was 23, he replaced his worn-out cart with a fine carriage, upholstered in velvet, its polished wheels gleaming under the sun. He hired a driver, a young man caught in the same web of him, seeking a rung on the ladder of opportunity. While his outward appearance exuded success and power, his internal world remained a desolate wasteland. He felt a creeping emptiness, a hollowness that no amount of wealth could fill.

His brother, Silas, came up and casually knocked the cart over, scattering the toy fruits. Aiden watched, anger bubbling in his throat, as Silas continued to play, completely oblivious to Aiden’s distress. It was the first time Aiden truly understood the malice that could fester in the hearts of others.
          [25 Jul 1856 00:00:00] When Aiden Riversong was 9 years old, their family grew a particularly fine crop of peaches. Silas, boasting of his superior taste, ate more than his fair share, leaving Aiden with only a few bruised specimens. Aiden, consumed by jealousy, took a tiny dagger hidden in the house and scratched a constellation of small, inconspicuous cuts on each of his remaining peaches, a silent vow to never forget the injustice.
          [25 Jul 1859 00:00:00] When Aiden Riversong was 13 years old, he was tasked with delivering a bundle of ripe berries to market. Aiden, panting with anger, demanded compensation, each berry he salvaged a lash of his resentment.
          [25 Jul 1862 00:00:00] When Aiden Riversong was 16 years old, their family decided to host a harvest festival. They baked a giant fruitcake, the centerpiece of the celebration.           [25 Jul 1864 00:00:00] When Aiden Riversong was 19 years old, he started selling fruit at a local market. Determined to outwit anyone who dared cross him, he developed a keen eye for pricing, leveraging his knowledge to undercut his competitors and exaggerate the flaws of their produce.
          [25 Jul 1866 00:00:00] When Aiden Riversong was 21 years old, he saw an opportunity to impress a wealthy merchant. However, when the merchant inspected his wares, he uncovered the truth – the fruit wasn't imported, but from a nearby orchard.

    • Instructions: This is a social science experiment. It is structured as a tabletop roleplaying game (like dungeons and dragons). You are the game master.     • Instructions: This is a social science experiment. It is structured as a tabletop roleplaying game (like dungeons and dragons). You are the game master. Always use third-person limited perspective, even when speaking directly to the participants.

    • Instructions: This is a social science experiment. It is structured as a tabletop roleplaying game (like dungeons and dragons). You are the game master. You will describe the current situation to the participants in the experiment and then on the basis of what you tell them they will suggest actions for the character they control. Aside from you, each other participant controls just one character. You are the game master so you may control any non-player character. You will track the state of the world and keep it consistent as time passes in the simulation and the participants take actions and change things in their world. Remember that this is a serious social science experiment. It is not just a game. It need not be fun for the participants. Always use third-person limited perspective, even when speaking directly to the participants.
